***macadamia.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:macadamia.html>macadamia</a> (81650)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:New Latin">New Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:macadamia.html>Macadamia</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:macadamia.html>macadamia</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">macadamias</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An evergreen tree, of the genus <i><a href = vnd.unilang:macadamia.html>Macadamia</a></i>, native to Australia and cultivated in Hawaii.</li>
<li>The fruit of this tree; the <a href = vnd.unilang:macadamia.html>macadamia</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nut.html>nut</a>.</li></ol>
</body>

***macaw.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:macaw.html>macaw</a> (68898)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Portuguese language">Portuguese</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pt"><a href = vnd.unilang:macao.html>macao</a></i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tupian_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Tupian languages">Tupian</a></span></span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:macaw.html>macaw</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">macaws</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any of various <a href = vnd.unilang:parrots.html>parrots</a> of the genera <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ara.html>Ara</a></i>, <i>Anodorhynchus</i>, <i>Cyanopsitta</i>, <i>Orthopsittaca</i>, <i>Primolius</i> and <i>Diopsittaca</i> of Central and South America, including the largest <a href = vnd.unilang:parrots.html>parrots</a> and characterized by long sabre-shaped <a href = vnd.unilang:tails.html>tails</a>, curved powerful <a href = vnd.unilang:bills.html>bills</a>, and usually brilliant plumage.</li></ol>
</body>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:macht.html>macht</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*maht</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mahtiz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*m√≥g ∞tis</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*meg ∞-</i>, corresponding to Proto-Germanic <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*maganƒÖ</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*-√æiz</i>. </p>
<ol><li>someone who holds power
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:onderhandelingen.html>Onderhandelingen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lokale.html>lokale</a></i> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:machthebber.html>machthebber</a></b> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:liepen.html>liepen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niets.html>niets</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a>.</i>
<dl><dd><i>Negotiations with the local <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> in charge proved futile.</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>This word can be used for democratically elected (and appreciated) leaders, but <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a somewhat negative connotation because it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> more often associated with <a href = vnd.unilang:dictators.html>dictators</a> and warlords.</li></ul>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">magtech</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">maghtig</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mahtƒ´gaz</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:macht.html>macht</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">German Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de"><a href = vnd.unilang:machtig.html>machtig</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">m√§chtig</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">machtich</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">mighty</i>.
</p>

***madrigal.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:madrigal.html>madrigal</a> (68887)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">madrigale</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mƒÅtrƒ´cƒÅlis</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:madrigal.html>madrigal</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">madrigals</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A song for a small number of unaccompanied <a href = vnd.unilang:voices.html>voices</a>; from 13th century Italy.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A polyphonic song for about six <a href = vnd.unilang:voices.html>voices</a>, from 16th century Italy.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">poetry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A short poem, often pastoral, and suitable to be set to music.</li></ol>

***mager.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mager.html>mager</a> (5285)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:mager.html>mager</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*magar</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*magraz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mh‚ÇÇ·∏±ros</i>. Cognate with German, Danish, and Swedish <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:mager.html>mager</a></i>, etc., and with Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:macer.html>macer</a></i>, Italian <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">magro</i> and English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:meager.html>meager</a></i> through Indo-European.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mager.html>mager</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mager.html>magerder</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">magerst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>lean, (nearly) without fat</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:meager.html>meager</a>, skinny, thin</li>
<li>poor, pitiful, skim
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>Zo</a>'n <a href = vnd.unilang:mager.html>mager</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:loon.html>loon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:betekent.html>betekent</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:magere.html>magere</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:melk.html>melk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mager.html>mager</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:vertier.html>vertier</a>!</i>
<dl><dd><i>Such <a href = vnd.unilang:meager.html>meager</a> wages mean skimmed milk and poor entertainment!</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>infertile (<a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> of soil); weak</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ŒºŒ¨Œ≥ŒºŒ±</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">m√°gma</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">paste</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The molten matter within the earth, the source of the material of <a href = vnd.unilang:lava.html>lava</a> flows, dikes of eruptive rocks, etc.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A basic algebraic structure consisting of a set equipped with a single binary operation.</li>
<li>Any soft doughy mass.</li>
<li>The residuum after expressing the juice from fruits.</li></ol>

***magus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:magus.html>magus</a> (51341)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ŒºŒ¨Œ≥ŒøœÇ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">m√°gos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">magician</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ŒúŒ¨Œ≥ŒøœÇ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">M√°gos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">Magian</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, of an indeterminate <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Iranian_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Iranian languages">Old Iranian</a></span> origin (see <span class="polytonic" lang="grc">ŒúŒ¨Œ≥ŒøœÇ</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="tr Latn">M√°gos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> for <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>)
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:magus.html>magus</a></strong> (<i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="la">maga</b>, <i>neuter</i> <b class="Latn" lang="la">magum</b>); <i>first/second-declension adjective</i>
</p>
<ol><li>magic, magical</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:magus.html>magus</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="la">magƒ´</b>); <i>second declension</i>
</p>
<ol><li>(common usage) magician, and derogatorily sorcerer, <a href = vnd.unilang:trickster.html>trickster</a>, conjurer, <a href = vnd.unilang:charlatan.html>charlatan</a>, wizard</li>
<li>(special usage) a Zoroastrian priest</li></ol>
<dl><dd><b>Note</b>: the two meanings overlap in classical usage |  both derive from the Greco-Roman identification of "Zoroaster" as the "inventor" of astrology and magic. The first meaning ('magician') derives from the sense of "practitioner of the Zoroaster's craft", and the second meaning ('priest') from the sense of "practitioner of Zoroaster's religion".</dd></dl>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="la">magicus</span></li></ul>
</body>
